
=================================================================
1-SHOT
With only the questionnaire TOPIC
=================================================================

-------------------
[SAMPLE] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1213249
     - Topic: Training effectiveness
     - Question number: 2

-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 {
"data": {
"TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
{
"CODE": "STRESSATWORK",
"NAME": "Stress at Work Questionnaire",
"_TF_QUESTIONS": [
{
"CODE": "Q1",
"NAME": "Do you feel that you have enough time to do everything that you need to do at work?",
"TYPE_ID": 3,
"DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
"_TF_ANSWERS": [
{"ANSWER": "Yes, I have enough time to do everything that I need to do at work."},
{"ANSWER": "No, I do not have enough time to do everything that I need to do at work."}
]
},
{
"CODE": "Q2",
"NAME": "Do you feel that the work that you do is ‘understood’ and appreciated by the organization?",
"TYPE_ID": 3,
"DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
"_TF_ANSWERS": [
{"ANSWER": "Yes, I feel that the work I do is understood and appreciated by the organization."},
{"ANSWER": "No, I do not feel that the work I do is understood and appreciated by the organization."}
]
},
{
"CODE": "Q3",
"NAME": "Do you feel that you are able to ‘turn off’ work-related thoughts, feelings, and worries when you leave the workplace?",
"TYPE_ID": 3,
"DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
"_TF_ANSWERS": [
{"ANSWER": "Yes, I am able to turn off work-related thoughts, feelings, and worries when I leave the workplace."},
{"ANSWER": "No, I find it difficult to turn off work-related thoughts, feelings, and worries when I leave the workplace."}
]
},
{
"CODE": "Q4",
"NAME": "Do you feel that you have control over the way you work and the decisions that you make?",
"TYPE_ID": 3,
"DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
"_TF_ANSWERS": [
{"ANSWER": "Yes, I feel that I have control over the way I work and the decisions that I make."},
{"ANSWER": "No, I do not feel that I have control over the way I work and the decisions that I make."}
]
},
{
"CODE": "Q5",
"NAME": "Do you feel that you are able to meet the demands of your work?",
"TYPE_ID": 3,
"DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
"_TF_ANSWERS": [
{"ANSWER": "Yes, I feel that I am able to meet the demands of my work."},
{"ANSWER": "No, I do not feel that I am able to meet the demands of my work."}
]
},
{
"CODE": "Q6",
"NAME": "Do you feel that the environment at work is ‘healthy’ and does not have a negative impact on your health?",
"TYPE_ID": 3,
"DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
"_TF_ANSWERS": [
{"ANSWER": "Yes, I feel that the environment at work is ‘healthy’ and does not have a negative impact on my health."},
{"ANSWER": "No, I do not feel that the environment at work is ‘healthy’ and that it has a negative impact on my health."}
]
},
{
"CODE": "Q7",
"NAME": "Do you feel that you are able to make a useful contribution to the organization?",
"TYPE_ID": 3,
"DISPLAY_ORDER": 7,
"_TF_ANSWERS": [
{"ANSWER": "Yes, I feel that I am able to make a useful contribution to the organization."},
{"ANSWER": "No, I do not feel that I am able to make a useful contribution to the organization."}
]
},
{
"CODE": "Q8",
"NAME": "Do you feel that the organization takes your needs into account when implementing changes?",
"TYPE_ID": 3,
"DISPLAY_ORDER": 8,
"_TF_ANSWERS": [
{"ANSWER": "Yes, I feel that the organization takes my needs into account when implementing changes."},
{"ANSWER": "No, I do not feel that the organization takes my needs into account when implementing changes."}
]
}
]
}
}

        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

[LLM ANSWER]
 "data": {"TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [{"CODE": "WORKPLACE_ENVIRONMENT_1", "NAME": "Workplace Environment Assessment", "_TF_QUESTIONS": [{"CODE": "Q1", "NAME": "How would you rate the overall cleanliness of your workplace?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Very clean"}, {"ANSWER": "Clean"}, {"ANSWER": "Neutral"}, {"ANSWER": "Dirty"}, {"ANSWER": "Very dirty"}]}, {"CODE": "Q2", "NAME": "How would you rate the availability of clean drinking water at your workplace?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Very clean"}, {"ANSWER": "Clean"}, {"ANSWER": "Neutral"}, {"ANSWER": "Dirty"}, {"ANSWER": "Very dirty"}]}, {"CODE": "Q3", "NAME": "How would you rate the temperature at your workplace?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Too cold"}, {"ANSWER": "Slightly cold"}, {"ANSWER": "Neutral"}, {"ANSWER": "Slightly warm"}, {"ANSWER": "Too warm"}]}, {"CODE": "Q4", "NAME": "How would you rate the noise level at your workplace?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Too noisy"}, {"ANSWER": "Slightly noisy"}, {"ANSWER": "Neutral"}, {"ANSWER": "Slightly quiet"}, {"ANSWER": "Very quiet"}]}, {"CODE": "Q5", "NAME": "How would you rate the amount of natural light in your workplace?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Too little"}, {"ANSWER": "Slightly less than ideal"}, {"ANSWER": "Neutral"}, {"ANSWER": "Slightly more than ideal"}, {"ANSWER": "Too much"}]}, {"CODE": "Q6", "NAME": "How would you rate the overall healthiness of your workplace?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Very healthy"}, {"ANSWER": "Healthy"}, {"ANSWER": "Neutral"}, {"ANSWER": "Unhealthy"}, {"ANSWER": "Very unhealthy"}]}, {"CODE": "Q7", "NAME": "What improvements would you suggest?", "TYPE_ID": 4, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 7, "_TF_ANSWERS": []}]}

With only the questionnaire TOPIC
=================================================================

-------------------
[SAMPLE] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100024
     - Topic: Internal Mobility Opportunities
     - Question number: 6

-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1173002
     - Topic: End of working relationship
     - Question number: 10
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on End of working relationship

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 "data": {"TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [{"CODE": "END_OF_WORKING_RELATIONSHIP", "NAME": "End of Working Relationship", "_TF_QUESTIONS": [{"CODE": "Q1", "NAME": "What was the reason for your departure from the company?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Retirement"}, {"ANSWER": "Voluntary termination"}, {"ANSWER": "Termination for cause"}, {"ANSWER": "Contract expiration, no renewal"}, {"ANSWER": "Health issues, unable to work"}]}, {"CODE": "Q2", "NAME": "Do you feel that your departure was handled properly by the company?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Yes, completely"}, {"ANSWER": "Yes, to some extent"}, {"ANSWER": "No, not really"}, {"ANSWER": "No, not at all"}]}, {"CODE": "Q3", "NAME": "Were you given the opportunity to provide feedback about your experience with the company?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Yes, completely"}, {"ANSWER": "Yes, to some extent"}, {"ANSWER": "No, not really"}, {"ANSWER": "No, not at all"}]}, {"CODE": "Q4", "NAME": "Were you satisfied with the communication and support received during your time with the company?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Yes, completely"}, {"ANSWER": "Yes, to some extent"}, {"ANSWER": "No, not really"}, {"ANSWER": "No, not at all"}]}, {"CODE": "Q5", "NAME": "If you could change one thing about your experience with the company, what would it be?", "TYPE_ID": 4, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5, "_TF_ANSWERS": []}]}]}

The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

Please explain this data and what is the purpose of this data

The data provided is a list of questions about career paths and opportunities within an organization. Each question is associated with a 5-level Likert scale, with options being Strongly agree, Somewhat agree, Neutral, Somewhat disagree, and Strongly disagree.

The purpose of these questions is to assess whether employees have a clear understanding of career paths, resources, and opportunities available within the organization. This can help organizations identify areas for improvement and provide better career development opportunities for their employees.

This looks like a list of questions or a survey about employee satisfaction and engagement. The questions seem to cover a range of topics, including job satisfaction, work-life balance, resources, autonomy, and alignment with personal values. It's important to have a satisfied and engaged workforce because it can lead to higher productivity, lower turnover, and better overall organizational performance. Here are some specific thoughts about this survey:

- The questions cover a wide range of topics, which can be both a strength and a weakness. On the one hand, it allows for a comprehensive understanding of an employee's experience, but on the other hand, it might be overwhelming, and the responses may be less accurate.

- The use of a 5-point Likert scale is a good idea because it allows for a more nuanced response than just "yes" or "no" and can capture a range of attitudes.

- It might be useful to add a few more open-ended, narrative-style questions to get a better sense of individual employee experiences and perspectives. For example, a question about what they like most about their job or what could be improved could provide valuable insights.

- It's also important to consider the timing and frequency of this survey. If it's conducted too often, employees may become fatigued and provide less thoughtful responses. If it's not conducted frequently enough, it might be difficult to track changes over time.

- The survey could be improved by including a question about diversity and inclusion in the workplace, as this is an important factor in employee satisfaction and engagement.

- Finally, it might be helpful to include a brief introduction and explanation of the survey to provide context and help employees feel more comfortable answering the questions. This could include the purpose of the survey, how the data will be used, and confidentiality guarantees.

This is a JSON representation of a questionnaire on the topic of "Employee Potential". The questions in this questionnaire are designed to assess how well an employee is being utilized and if their potential is being fully realized in their current role. The questionnaire also asks about job satisfaction, education level, and whether the employee's employer supports their career growth.

The questionnaire includes the following questions:
1. What is your current job title?
2. How would you rate your current job satisfaction?
3. Do you feel that you are being utilized to your full potential in your current role?
4. What level of education do you have?

 "data": {"TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [{"CODE": "FEEDBACK_MECHANISMS_1", "NAME": "Feedback Mechanisms", "_TF_QUESTIONS": [{"CODE": "Q1", "NAME": "How do you prefer to give feedback to your team members?", "TYPE_ID": 3, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "In person"}, {"ANSWER": "Email"}, {"ANSWER": "Meeting"}, {"ANSWER": "Phone call"}]}, {"CODE": "Q2", "NAME": "Do you prefer to give positive or negative feedback first?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Positive"}, {"ANSWER": "Negative"}]}, {"CODE": "Q3", "NAME": "What do you think about the importance of feedback in a team's success?", "TYPE_ID": 3, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Very important"}, {"ANSWER": "Important"}, {"ANSWER": "Neutral"}, {"ANSWER": "Not important"}, {"ANSWER": "Very unimportant"}]}, {"CODE": "Q4", "NAME": "What is your preferred method of receiving feedback?", "TYPE_ID": 3, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "In person"}, {"ANSWER": "Email"}, {"ANSWER": "Meeting"}, {"ANSWER": "Phone call"}]}, {"CODE": "Q5", "NAME": "Do you think that feedback should be given regularly or only during performance evaluations?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Regularly"}, {"ANSWER": "Only during evaluations"}]}, {"CODE": "Q6", "NAME": "How do you feel about giving feedback to your direct manager?", "TYPE_ID": 3, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Very comfortable"}, {"ANSWER": "Somewhat comfortable"}, {"ANSWER": "Neutral"}, {"ANSWER": "Somewhat uncomfortable"}, {"ANSWER": "Very uncomfortable"}]}, {"CODE": "Q7", "NAME": "What is your preferred method of receiving negative feedback?", "TYPE_ID": 3, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 7, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "In person"}, {"ANSWER": "Email"}, {"ANSWER": "Meeting"}, {"ANSWER": "Phone call"}]}, {"CODE": "Q8", "NAME": "Do you think that feedback should be given anonymously?", "TYPE_ID": 1, "DISPLAY_ORDER": 8, "_TF_ANSWERS": [{"ANSWER": "Yes"}, {"ANSWER": "No"}]}]}]}}

This questionnaire includes questions about how feedback is given and received, as well as the importance of feedback in a team's success. The questions also address whether feedback should be given regularly or only during performance evaluations, and if it should be given anonymously. The preferred methods of giving and receiving feedback are also explored, including in person, through email, in a meeting, or on the phone. The question about giving feedback to a direct manager is also included.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

     - User:

            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.

            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.

 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.

 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.

     - Question number: 4

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100018
     - Topic: Feedback Mechanisms
     - Question number: 9
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

This can include things like bullying, discrimination, or other forms of harassment, as well as more overtly harmful activities like torture or abuse. It can also refer to situations that cause stress, anxiety, or burnout. The question is asking whether the workplace has enough measures in place to prevent or mitigate these types of psychologically harmful situations.

If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

This JSON object represents a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities. It has one questionnaire with five questions. The questions are asking about the availability and distribution of internal mobility opportunities, as well as the opinions and suggestions for improvement from employees. The questionnaire code is "INTERNAL\_MOBILITY\_OPPORTUNITIES\_3" and the name is "Internal Mobility Opportunities". The questions are displayed in order and have a type\_id, display\_order, and a list of possible answers. The type\_id indicates the type of question, and the display\_order indicates the order in which the questions should be displayed. The _TF\_ANSWERS array is used to capture the responses to the questions. The final two questions allow for open-ended responses to capture more detailed opinions and suggestions.

            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

     - User:

The display order determines the order in which the questions should be displayed, and the code is a unique identifier for each question.

2. The leader helps team members overcome their obstacles.
3. The leader provides safety and protection.

6. The leader empowers others.
7. The leader is supportive and understanding.

10. The leader is confident in their decision making.
11. The leader is open to new ideas.
12. The leader is able to admit their mistakes.
13. The leader is able to create a feeling of safety and belonging within the team.
14. The leader is able to use power and authority to silence or ignore others.
15. The leader is able to seek out opportunities for professional development.
16. The leader is able to adapt to change and encourage innovation within the team.
17. The leader is able to establish clear roles and responsibilities within the team.
18. The leader is able to support and represent the team when interacting with other departments and individuals.
19. The leader is able to inspire a shared vision and sense of purpose within the team.
20. The leader is able to enable others to feel powerful and in control.
21. The leader is able to create a feeling of safety and belonging within the team.
22. The leader is able to use power and authority to silence or ignore others.
23. The leader is able to seek out opportunities for professional development.
24. The leader is able to adapt to change and encourage innovation within the team.
25. The leader is able to establish clear roles and responsibilities within the team.

These statements can be used to evaluate the leadership qualities of a person. A leader who scores highly on these statements is likely to be a good leader.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

I think that if an employer prioritized work-life balance, it would create a better work environment and lead to happier, more productive employees.

19) Alice, do you feel that you have enough time to do everything you want to do?

I do not feel that I have enough time to do everything I want to do. With the demands of work, family, and personal responsibilities, it's challenging to find time for everything that I want to do. I prioritize my tasks and use time management techniques to ensure that I am dedicating time to what's most important to me.

20) Do you feel that technology and communication tools are intrusive and disrupt your work-life balance?

I do not believe that technology and communication tools are inherently intrusive or disruptive. Instead, they can be used as tools to create a better work-life balance. The real challenge is setting boundaries and being intentional about using technology and communication tools in a way that supports my well-being.

21) Alice, do you feel that you have a good work-life balance?

I do not feel that I have a good work-life balance. With the demands of work, family, and personal responsibilities, it's challenging to find the right balance. I prioritize taking breaks and setting boundaries to ensure that I am performing at my best and have a good work-life balance.

22) Do you feel that you have the necessary resources to maintain a healthy work-life balance?

I do not feel that I have the necessary resources to maintain a healthy work-life balance. While there may be policies and resources in place, I do not feel that they are sufficient to create a better work-life balance. I think that if an employer prioritized work-life balance, it would create a better work environment and lead to happier, more productive employees.

23) Alice, do you feel that you have enough time to relax and recharge?

I do not feel that I have

            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.

The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
